msg:Before I went, I was hesitant about whether to choose Jinglan. I read the bad reviews and hesitated for a long time. I booked several hotels and then canceled them. Finally, I decided on Jinglan. In general, I made a good choice. If you stay in Gaozhuang, you should choose this place. Regular hotel facilities and services, lobby, breakfast, swimming pool, hot spring, gym are all online. There is nothing wrong with the accommodation room in the West Tower. Although it looks a bit old, the bedding is very comfortable and sleep-friendly. There are small bottles of toiletries from L'Occitane, and there are only four bottles of mineral water for drinks, no coke or anything. The sixth floor has a platform with a quiet mountain view. Both the elderly and children like it. There is only one staff member to check in, which is not good. You need to queue up, which does not match the image of this hotel. The lemongrass water in the lobby is delicious, but I doubt whether the cups are cleaned. It is reasonable to replace them with disposable paper cups. The Xingguang Night Market is very lively. Be careful to avoid scams. You will be ripped off by the barbecue. A bunch of beef skewers are small. When checking out, they said 4 yuan for a small skewer and 38 skewers for a bunch. In Harbin, small skewers are sold by the bunch for 20 or 30 yuan. It's my fault for not asking clearly... A barbecue meal that didn't fill you up cost 518. The fruits in Gaozhuang are also very expensive. Kirin watermelon, which was 6 yuan in my Northeast, costs 9.8 per pound there. Business in Xishuangbanna is not very friendly to tourists. Of course, it is also possible that all the shops are opened by outsiders.

The corridors and rooms are carpeted, and there is a musty smell, especially in the room. The bathroom also smells bad, and the sanitation is not cleaned carefully. The pants drying on the balcony are covered with a layer of dust. We booked three rooms, one of which has an exhaust fan that cannot be turned off and makes noises all night. The sound insulation is not good, and the flushing upstairs can be heard very clearly downstairs.
The breakfast is particularly bad. There are so many people like a vegetable market. There is no waiter to lead the seat. You need to grab it yourself or share a table with others. The food is almost all semi-finished, and the quality is the worst in this product. The breakfast is written until 10:30, but in fact, eggs are no longer available from 9:30, and fruits are not added.
There is an infinity pool on the fifth floor, but it cannot be put into the water in winter. There are several hot spring pools that are OK.
The only advantage of the whole hotel is that it is a 200-meter walk from the Starlight Night Market. If you want to be close to the night market, you can stay in the cheaper East Tower. There is no need to pay double the price for the West Tower, because the facilities and front desk of the East and West Towers are the same. The West Tower is under the name of hotel management, but the actual operation is not as good as a serviced apar**ent or a chain of express hotels.
The hotel has a beautiful appearance and a good location, but the rest is too ordinary. It is the only mine in Banna.

Apart from looking resplendent, it really has no special features.
